href=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?a=kJYgD06yn7o:HlqlA17Jjt8:qj6IDK7rITs\"><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=qj6IDK7rITs\" border=\"0\"></img></a> <a href=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?a=kJYgD06yn7o:HlqlA17Jjt8:gIN9vFwOqvQ\"><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=kJYgD06yn7o:HlqlA17Jjt8:gIN9vFwOqvQ\" border=\"0\"></img></a>\n</div><img src=\"http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/businessinsider/~4/kJYgD06yn7o\" height=\"1\" width=\"1\" alt=\"\"/>","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Sun, 04 Apr 2021 14:59:06 +0000","feedId":22,"bgimg":"https://i.insider.com/6069bd1ba7d803001963ea81?format=jpeg","linkMd5":"a9aed59c4b52ccc99297de835de94100","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn31@2020_6/2021/04/05/06-46-03-185_2ba5cba824592add.webp","destWidth":1200,"destHeight":900,"sourceBytes":58656,"destBytes":58656,"author":"sankel@businessinsider.com (Sophia Ankel)","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://i.insider.com/6069bd2fa7d803001963ea83?format=jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx22/cdn77@2020_3/2021/04/05/06-46-10-138_6d00e3b9b16f1ae7.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=yIl2AUoC8zA":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn6@2020_6/2021/04/05/06-46-09-303_cc3ef43fc8ff5801.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=kJYgD06yn7o:HlqlA17Jjt8:F7zBnMyn0Lo":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx8/cdn45@2020_5/2021/04/05/06-46-09-614_f31ddf6154fd2f69.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=kJYgD06yn7o:HlqlA17Jjt8:V_sGLiPBpWU":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx25/cdn20@2020_1/2021/04/05/06-46-04-091_11502045150cde78.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?d=qj6IDK7rITs":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx22/cdn97@2020_3/2021/04/05/06-46-06-748_740defb435ea442b.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~ff/businessinsider?i=kJYgD06yn7o:HlqlA17Jjt8:gIN9vFwOqvQ":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn49@2020_6/2021/04/05/06-46-10-260_365a4e083dfd7b53.webp","http://feeds.feedburner.com/~r/businessinsider/~4/kJYgD06yn7o":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx1/cdn25@2020_1/2021/04/05/06-46-05-587_fea215f743c3e42c.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1617605114850},{"createdTime":"2021-04-05 14:45:14","updatedTime":"2021-04-05 14:45:14","title":"The case for a no-strings-attached monthly payment to help families get back on their feet after the pandemic, according to an economic security expert","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/seed-program-stockton-california-guaranteed-income-benefits-marginalized-families-2021-3","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6054bc43a7446d0018c8514c?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Jobless claims\" height=\"1666\" width=\"2222\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Guaranteed income helps stabilize people during difficult times such as during a pandemic.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Bryan Woolston/Reuters</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Natalie Foster is the cofounder of the Economic Security Project, a network dedicated to advancing a guaranteed income in America.</li>\n<li>The following is an excerpt from her contribution to the anthology, <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/New-Possible-Visions-beyond-Crisis-ebook/dp/B08KFSNG1Q\">The New Possible: Visions of Our World Beyond Crisis</a>.</li>\n<li>She says in the wake of COVID-19, economic resilience can be part of our reality through guaranteed income.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>Guaranteed income is a robust response to so many contradictions.</p><p>We see the benefits of divorcing work from worth playing out in Stockton, California. Mayor Michael Tubbs, the first Black mayor elected to office at the ripe age of  26, is running a guaranteed income pilot. He makes the case that poverty comes from a lack of cash, not a lack of character.</p><p>We knew providing a stable income was important pre-pandemic, but post-pandemic it is a lifeline for Stockton families. Guaranteed income helps these families weather the crisis with more resilience than their neighbors.</p><p>I can&#39;t help but imagine how this approach could have helped millions more if it had been part of our economic approach across the country. What would it mean to have this kind of an economic floor?</p><p>Named the Stockton Economic Empowerment Demonstration (SEED), the program gives 125 families in Stockton an income floor of $500 a month for 18 months. The income is unconditional. This means there are no strings attached and no work requirements.</p><p>Stockton is a city in the process of reinventing itself, with no shortage of challenges. It was the largest city to go bankrupt after the last financial crisis. It&#39;s a city that is representative of America, with a majority of the population being people of color. One in four Stocktonians live in poverty; the median income is around $44,000.</p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6054bd5a1fcb5700186ee62b?format=jpeg\" alt=\"book 553x677\" height=\"677\" width=\"553\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>The New Possible anthology.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Natalie Foster et al</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><p>The families participating in the guaranteed income pilot provide compelling data for how cash transfers allow families to remain resilient in the face of a pandemic. In these families, we see how no-strings-attached cash provides a way forward in economic uncertainty.</p><p>That resilience is the promise of the SEED project in particular, and the promise of guaranteed income more broadly.</p><h2>To see the impact on people&#39;s lives, let&#39;s look at one recipient&#39;s story.</h2><p>For Tomas, the outbreak happened as he was getting his security clearance for a job at the airport. As with many companies, the pandemic caused a hiring freeze and halted the application process at the airport.</p><p>Suddenly finding himself out of work and without any jobless benefits, the guaranteed income became Tomas&#39; sole financial fallback.</p><p>Tomas can&#39;t live on $500 or even $1,000 a month, but the guaranteed income is not meant to be an income on its own. It supports resilience. It works to stabilize the erratic ups and downs and to help people through difficult times in times of widespread destabilization. This is something we should all have, and our current political and economic moment makes it a possibility. We can make this kind of economic care and resilience part of our reality in the wake of COVID-19.</p><p>We are often asked, &#34;What do people spend the money on?&#34; The answer: People spend the money on food, general supplies, and utilities. But wanting to know exactly where the money goes misses the point. A more interesting question is: &#34;What does the money do?&#34; The evidence shows that meaningful psychological and emotional gains are embedded in providing people with the resources to take care of their basic needs.</p><p>Researchers Dr. Amy Castro Baker and Dr. Stacia West, who are independently evaluating the Stockton program, understand this point. Beyond tracking the basics of where the money goes, they are evaluating questions of wellbeing, including stress levels, hope, and feelings of belonging. The two researchers define hope in the way that they ask the question: &#34;Do you want to wake up in the morning?&#34; Hope is about goals, pathways, and agency. As Dr. Castro Baker puts it, &#34;Keep in mind - the opposite of hope is despair. Understanding how economic security is linked to hope is key. Many would argue that change and justice are simply not possible without hope.&#34;</p><p>They also ask interviewees, &#34;Do you feel seen? Do you feel seen as a human being by institutions with power over your life?&#34; If you don&#39;t feel like you matter as a human, your capacity for hope is limited. Hope is one of the most significant predictors of whether or not you will engage with positive and healthy interventions when capitalism has already spit you out, or when it has communicated to you that you do not serve a purpose.</p><p>According to Dr. Castro Baker, &#34;Hope is about saying: To what degree can a justice-based intervention such as a guaranteed income serve as a financial vaccine in a prolonged stressful environment with an unknown end?&#34;</p><p>Early trends indicate that, with just $500 cash a month, people can move the needle on both hope and belonging. </p><figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6069c545856cd700198a3135?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Natalie Foster\" height=\"1345\" width=\"1794\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Natalie Foster.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Tyler Driscoll</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><h2>Better Ideas Aren&#39;t Necessarily New Ideas</h2><p>It has been heartening to see guaranteed income percolate into Stockton society as a possible response to the pandemic and the treacherous economic insecurity experienced by so many Americans. Giving people cash works. I</p><p>t&#39;s not a new idea; Dr. Martin Luther King Jr. also spoke and wrote extensively on the power of a guaranteed income. He was pushed in his thinking by activists such as Johnnie Tillmon, who played a critical role in the National Welfare Rights Organization.</p><p>Nearly 50 years ago Johnnie Tillmon, a welfare rights advocate, wrote, &#34;The truth is, a job doesn&#39;t necessarily mean an adequate income. There are some ten million jobs that now pay less than the minimum wage, and if you&#39;re a woman, you&#39;ve got the best chance of getting one.&#34;  Tillmon&#39;s words are still true today. </p><p>As a result of the pandemic, more and more Americans experience low wages, income insecurity, degrading interactions with benefits offices, and lack of protections. While these have been the consistent experience of many Black Americans, the blacklight is exposing others to this harsh reality as well. The extraordinary economic disruption is now moving beyond the segregated zip codes, where it has lingered untended for far too long.</p><p>While the impacts of the coronavirus mean that more people now experience economic inequality, people of color have been advocating for economic justice for decades. We now have an opportunity and a responsibility to advance new rules with old roots in a meaningful way right now.</p><p>Even in a short amount of time, we&#39;ve made tremendous strides. When I cofounded the Economic Security Project, guaranteed income struck people as a far-fetched idea and even a pipe dream. But that just isn&#39;t the case anymore.</p><p>The uncomfortable truth is that there will be future pandemics - whether they are the result of climate change, job automation, or something entirely unforeseen. We will find ourselves here again. But let&#39;s make sure that, when that day comes, the economic realities of American families are in a very different place. Right now, we can begin to offer the economic resilience required to weather these changes and the turmoil they bring.</p><p>As a nation, there is still much reckoning to be done. But we can&#39;t be an anti-racist, just society until we have safe and stable families and communities. And for this we need cash. Let&#39;s first provide a guaranteed income to stabilize every family. Then we can get to the hard work of healing this nation together.</p><p><em>This excerpt is adapted from <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/New-Possible-Visions-beyond-Crisis-ebook/dp/B08KFSNG1Q\">The New Possible: Visions of Our World Beyond Crisis</a>, published by Cascade Books, an imprint Wipf and Stock Publishers.</em></p><p><em>Natalie Foster is the president and cofounder of the Economic Security Project, a network dedicated to advancing a guaranteed income in America and reining in the unprecedented concentration of corporate power. </em></p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a href='https://www.businessinsider.com/seed-program-stockton-california-guaranteed-income-benefits-marginalized-families-2021-3'>Business Insider</a></div><div Easter greetings to you and your family. As we celebrate this most holy day, we know many are still going without familiar comforts of the season,&#34; the president said. &#34;The virus is not gone, and so many of us feel the longing and loneliness of distance. For a second year, most will be apart from their families, their friends, full congregations that fill us with joy.&#34;</p><p>&#34;Yet as the Gospel of John reminds us, the light shines in the darkness, and the darkness has not overcome it,&#34; he added.</p><blockquote class=\"twitter-tweet blockquote\" data-lang=\"en\" data-cards=\"\" data-conversation=\"\">-The Hill  (@thehill) <a href=\"https://twitter.com/mims/statuses/1378743161929928707?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw\">April 4, 2021</a></blockquote><script async=\"\" src=\"//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js\" charset=\"utf-8\"></script><p>The first lady echoed the president&#39;s remarks, adding that she&#39;s optimistic about the future of the United States in relation to economic downfalls and medical issues brought on by the coronavirus pandemic. </p><p>&#34;Today, as spring returns, we see hope all around us,&#34; she said. &#34;Families are getting the financial help they need to take a breath once again. More than 554,000 Americans have died from it. So far, about 56 million Americans, or 17%, have been fully vaccinated, according to JHU data. </p></section><p>The statement from the Bidens directly contrasts the <a 14:45:14","updatedTime":"2021-04-05 14:45:14","title":"Investors should buy real assets - from wine to art - as inflation reaches a 'secular turning point,' Bank of America says","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/stock-market-outlook-real-assets-inflation-hedge-portfolio-investing-wine-2021-4","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60662d76902281001950aad5?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Art Gallery\" height=\"512\" width=\"1024\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>\n<p class=\"copyright\">Oli Scarff/Getty Images</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul>\n<li style=\"list-style-type: none;\" aria-level=\"1\">\n<ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li><strong>Bank of America forecasts an uptick in inflation and that rates will weigh on stock returns for the next decade. </strong></li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><strong>The bank&#39;s chief investment strategist says investors should buy real assets to hedge against inflation. </strong></li>\n<li><strong>Real assets are at their lowest point relative to financial assets in almost 100 years, he writes. </strong></li>\n<li><strong><a href=\"https://newsletter.businessinsider.com/join/4np/10-things-opening-bell?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingest?utm_source=markets&utm_medium=ingestedium=ingest\">Sign up here for our daily newsletter, 10 Things Before the Opening Bell</a></strong></li>\n</ul>\n</li>\n</ul><p>Since the election of President Joe Biden, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/us-economy-rebound-goods-commodities-services-more-expensive-inflation-stimulus-2021-2\">inflation and its potential comeback</a> have been <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/inflation-fears-wall-street-main-street-reopening-stimulus-economic-recovery-2021-3\">hot economic topics</a>. Pumping trillions of dollars into the economy could overheat it, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/inflation-stimulus-debate-economic-growth-spending-federal-reserve-larry-summers-2021-3\">critics say</a>, while <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/inflation-fears-biden-stimulus-package-misplaced-history-suggests-larry-summers-2021-1\">others see few signs</a> of runaway inflation, either now or in the near future.</p><p>Freak events in early 2021 like <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/texas-power-grid-failure-economist-galbraith-left-leaning-utility-deregulation-2021-2\">the Texas freeze</a> and the <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/suez-canal-blockage-us-gas-prices-oil-market-inflation-2021-3\">giant ship stuck in the Suez Canal</a> haven&#39;t clarified the issue, as they contributed to <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/more-expensive-goods-supply-shortage-congested-shipping-ports-texas-freeze-2021-3\">inflationary shocks</a> that <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/real-estate-homebuying-soaring-lumber-prices-new-homes-construction-2021-3\">may be &#34;transitory&#34;</a> or may not be.</p><p>Bank of America&#39;s chief investment strategist, Michael Hartnett, has seen enough to declare a &#34;<a href=\"https://markets.businessinsider.com/news/stocks/stock-market-outlook-inflation-stimulus-returns-bonds-investing-sectors-bofa-2021-3-1030175296#:~:text=Bank%20of%20America%20sees%202021,real%20assets%20against%20this%20backdrop.\">secular turning point</a>&#34; on inflation and anticipates that stock market returns will be lackluster over the next decade. Stock investors who&#39;ve seen a roughly 10% annual return from recent decades should expect that gain to go down to 3% to 5% over the course of the 2020s, he added.</p><p>But he has a recommendation: Real assets are a more overlooked part of the market that may offer investors protection against inflation while diversifying their portfolios.</p><p>In a recent note Hartnett said that real estate, commodities, and even collectibles like wine, art, diamonds, and cars could outperform in the next decade. Investors don&#39;t need to own the physical assets, Hartnett added, but instead can own REITs, and specialized funds that focus on these assets. </p><p>Real assets are positively correlated with inflation and interest rates, unlike financial assets like stocks and bonds, Hartnett said. During <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/millennials-boomers-inflation-fears-age-gap-stimulus-economic-growth-recovery-2021-3\">&#34;the Great Inflation&#34; of </a><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/millennials-boomers-inflation-fears-age-gap-stimulus-economic-growth-recovery-2021-3\">the</a><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/millennials-boomers-inflation-fears-age-gap-stimulus-economic-growth-recovery-2021-3\"> 1970s</a>, real estate and commodities outperformed large cap stocks and government bonds. He added that in eras where bonds and stocks struggle, real assets have provided superior risk-adjusted returns.</p><p>Over the past 5 and 10 years as inflation fell to the lowest average levels since the 1960s, real assets have seen lower returns and lower volatility, according to BofA data. Now, the price of real assets relative to financial assets are at the lowest point since 1925, making them attractive investments according to Hartnett.</p><p>Real assets are also underowned, with only 5.5% of the total market cap of all ETFs exposed to real assets. </p><p>Additionally, since 1926, collectibles (8.1%) and commodities (6.3%) have offered higher returns than government bonds (6.0%) and cash (3.4%), albeit with higher volatility.</p><p>Bank of America suggested investors seek out funds like the Fine Art Group, Classic Car Fund, and the London International Vintners Exchange Fine Wine Fund Index (FWIFFWID), in addition to REITs and commodity funds if they&#39;re looking for real asset exposure.</p><p><em><strong>Read more:</strong> <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/stock-picks-to-buy-with-best-profitability-growth-estimates-gs-2021-4\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener\">Goldman Sachs says buy these 33 stocks now as profits rebound for companies that suffered the most during the pandemic</a></em></p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a now operates transcontinental flights from numerous East Coast cities. It's not as big as the majors in the big four US airlines including American Airlines, Delta Air Lines, United Airlines, and Southwest Airlines, but Alaska has been getting its name out there in a big way.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b5b550d155e0019ef6713?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tMiddle seats on Alaska flights were blocked until January 7, the second-longest seat-blocking tenure of a major US airline behind Delta. Now, flights can be filled nearly to capacity in economy.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b9253106eb50019d056c1?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tHere's what flying Alaska Airlines is like during the pandemic.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b946e0d155e0019ef68c4?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1404\" width=\"1872\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tAlaska's primary hub at Seattle-Tacoma International Airport was busier than I expected when I arrived for my Friday afternoon flight to Los Angeles. As the airport's top carrier, many of those flyers would be flying Alaska.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b5e100d155e0019ef673c?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1665\" width=\"2220\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tThe entire Alaska Airlines check-in, however, had been overhauled with new safety features like plexiglass partitions at the counters...\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b947c0d155e0019ef68c6?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1410\" width=\"1880\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tSocial distancing placards in queues...\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b94880d155e0019ef68c7?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1665\" width=\"2221\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tHand sanitizer stations...\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b948e0d155e0019ef68c8?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1666\" width=\"2223\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tAnd wipe stations in between check-in kiosks. It was an impressive start to my trip on the airline.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b9498106eb50019d056db?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1398\" width=\"1865\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tAnd before I even got to the airport, I was required to acknowledge a health agreement. Standard for most major US airlines now, I had to affirm that I haven't tested positive for COVID-19 within the past 10 days, hadn't been exposed to the virus in the past 10 days, and hadn't exhibited symptoms in the past three days, in addition to agreeing to the airline's mask policy.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b949e0d155e0019ef68c9?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1202\" width=\"1603\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tThe flight appeared to be largely empty and it was looking good that I'd have a row to myself. Alaska flies near-hourly between Seattle and Los Angeles so there was no shortage of flights available, even during the pandemic.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b6f7e0d155e0019ef67da?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1513\" width=\"2017\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tI quickly got my ticket from the kiosk and headed to the gate. I hadn't flown on Alaska since before the pandemic when I flew from New York to LA to get In-n-Out Burger, so I was excited to fly the airline once more.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b94b00d155e0019ef68cb?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1427\" width=\"1903\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><strong><em>Read More: </em></strong><em><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/trip-to-la-for-plane-watching-and-in-n-out-burger-2020-2\" data-analytics-position=\"2\" data-analytics-module=\"\">I flew from New York to LA and back in a single day just to eat a cheeseburger and gawk at planes &#8211; here's why I'd do it again</a></em></p>\n\tThe same set of social distancing measures that I found at check-in were also at the gate, including more plexiglass partitions, hand sanitizing stations, and floor placards.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b5b48106eb50019d0551e?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tThe airport also had its own social distancing agenda, blocking every other seat in the gate area with placards.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b5b5a0d155e0019ef6718?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tBut while I had hoped for an empty flight, it turned out that this afternoon flight to Los Angeles was very popular with airline employees and standby passengers. There were at least 25 people looking to jump on board this flight, potentially thwarting my chances of an empty row.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b60430d155e0019ef6758?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1666\" width=\"2222\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tBoarding began around 30 minutes prior to departure with Alaska following its normal boarding procedure. Customers board with their assigned group, listed on their boarding passes.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b60650d155e0019ef675b?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1406\" width=\"1875\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tAfter pre-boarding, first class boards first followed by Alaska elites and those seated in \"premium class.\" Regular economy passengers in the back of the plane then board followed by those closer to the front. Basic economy flyers, regardless of seat location, board dead last.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b7287106eb50019d055fe?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1674\" width=\"2232\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying Alaska Airlines during the pandemic.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tMore social distancing placards lined the jetway leading up to the aircraft. \"Mind your wingspan\" is Alaska's slogan of choice for social distancing.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b60b3106eb50019d05579?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1392\" width=\"1857\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tFlight attendants welcomed us as we filed into the Boeing 737 Max but nothing in the way of hand sanitizer or sanitary wipes were offered, as some other airlines are doing.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b60bf106eb50019d0557a?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1459\" width=\"1946\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tWalking past first class, however, I noticed each seat was given hand sanitizing wipes, a perk that economy class didn't get.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b7606106eb50019d0561a?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tI later saw on the airline's website that they were available \"on request.\"\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b75fe0d155e0019ef67fd?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><em>Source: <a href=\"https://www.alaskaair.com/content/advisories/coronavirus/flying-during-covid\">Alaska Airlines</a></em></p>\n\tThe plane was spotless, however, as is to be expected since this was a brand-new plane that only began flying for Alaska a few days prior.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b76070d155e0019ef6800?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tAlaska, like most airlines, disinfects aircraft using electrostatic spraying, or \"fogging.\"\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b760a0d155e0019ef6804?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><em><strong>Read More: </strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/delta-united-american-are-fogging-planes-2020-4\">Delta, United, and American are 'fogging' their planes to make them safe for travel amid coronavirus &#8212; here's what that means</a></em></p>\n\tAircraft are also cleaned by crews before each flight, the airline says.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b76080d155e0019ef6802?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><em>Source: <a href=\"https://www.alaskaair.com/content/advisories/coronavirus/flying-during-covid\">Alaska Airlines</a></em></p>\n\tThe cleaning measures truly showed. I had no concerns whatsoever about the cleanliness of the plane.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b7617106eb50019d0562e?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tI chose seat 28F for the two-hour flight to Los Angeles, a window seat on the right side of the plane facing forward.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b76090d155e0019ef6803?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tEverything from the seat area to the tray tables was spotless.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b761c106eb50019d05630?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tAlaska even had some of its new safety protocols listed in this booklet with a website link where flyers could view the full spread of measures being taken by the airline to keep passengers safe.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b7617106eb50019d0562c?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tThis flight would feature an in-flight drink and snack service with nine different hot and cold beverages on offer ranging from Coke to orange juice.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b7612106eb50019d05626?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tThe rest of the plane slowly filled up and Alaska's boarding procedure meant the front filled out before the back. Those boarding last would have to walk through an entire plane full of people if they were seated in the back.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b760a106eb50019d0561f?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1874\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tFlight attendants during the boarding process continually reminded passengers that they were \"obligated\" to wear a face mask.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b760b106eb50019d05620?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tOne flight attendant was also walking around with masks to give to flyers that needed.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b760e106eb50019d05622?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tEven the safety briefing included a reminder that wearing a mask while flying is now federal law. Passengers were asked to report any offenses to flight attendants.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b761c106eb50019d05631?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tThe flight departed with quite a few middle seats open. Alaska doesn't currently block middle seats in regular economy as of January 7 so having any seats open was pure luck.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b7615106eb50019d05628?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tFlight attendants also worked to space passengers by moving them into empty rows. The aisle seat in my row, for example, was given to a passenger that was in a crowded row.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b7610106eb50019d05624?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tSoon enough, we were airborne and bound for Los Angeles.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b5b53106eb50019d05528?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tFlight attendants quickly began the in-flight service, starting with snacks.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b761a106eb50019d0562f?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tThe bag included a variety of items from pretzels to flaxseed chips.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b760f106eb50019d05623?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tThen the drink cart came around and gloved flight attendants distributed full beverage cans accompanied by a cup of ice and hand sanitizing wipes. Printed on the napkin was a message asking flyers to put their masks on between bites and sips.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b7615106eb50019d05629?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tOnce the service was over, I took a walk around the plane and only found a few passengers flouting the mask rule. Compliance, for the most part, was good.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b7617106eb50019d0562a?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tAlaska also isn't afraid to ban passengers for not wearing a mask. Almost 450 flyers have been banned as of March 17.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b7615106eb50019d05627?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t<p><em><strong>Read More: </strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/number-of-people-banned-by-us-airlines-not-wearing-mask-2021-1\">Airlines have banned more than 2,500 passengers for not wearing masks &#8212; here are the carriers that have booted the most</a></em></p>\n\tThe rest of the flight was spent enjoying the views of the West Coast as we headed towards Los Angeles.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b5b510d155e0019ef670e?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tAlaska, overall, has largely returned to normal when it comes to things like boarding and the in-flight service. I was surprised to see how much was on offer compared to other airlines.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b5b4c0d155e0019ef6709?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tI was also impressed by the airline's investment in social distancing measures at its Seattle hub, with everything from hand sanitizing stations to floor placards.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b5b4d0d155e0019ef670a?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tAnd even though it meant I didn't get the row to myself, I appreciated flight attendants being proactive in moving people around to distance flyers when possible.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b5b58106eb50019d0552c?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tThe routine flight down the coast was largely uneventful and soon enough, it was time to land in Los Angeles.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b5b69106eb50019d05540?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tAfter we landed, flight attendants reminded passengers to social distance when deplaning.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b5b50106eb50019d05523?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tBut most passengers just wanted off and didn't mind crowding the aisle, as is normal when flying regardless of whether there's an ongoing pandemic.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b760d0d155e0019ef6807?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas it","link":"https://www.businessinsider.com/republicans-covid-19-relief-bill-benefits-opposition-2021-4","description":"<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6069ea97a7d803001963ea93?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Madison Cawthorn\" height=\"1582\" width=\"2811\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Rep. Madison Cawthorn (R-North Carolina) speaks on the House floor.\n<p class=\"copyright\">House Television via AP</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>Republicans are touting benefits of the COVID-19 relief legislation they opposed in Congress.</li>\n<li>Mitch McConnell said Republicans would have a &#34;talk&#34; with Americans about the bill&#39;s issues.</li>\n<li>Meanwhile, funding for healthcare and restaurants is being praised by some GOP members.</li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul><p>For months, Congressional Republicans have been unanimously opposed to the <a href=\"https://www.congress.gov/bill/117th-congress/house-bill/1319/text\">American Rescue Plan Act of 2021</a>, the $1.9 trillion COVID-19 relief package that was backed by President Joe Biden and <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/stimulus-biden-signs-trillion-covid-relief-package-checks-direct-payments-2021-3\">signed into law</a> in March.</p><p>The stimulus package, which included $1,400 direct stimulus payments for individuals, funding for state and local governments, $300 in federal unemployment aid through September, and an expansion of the child tax credit, among other measures, did not receive a single GOP vote of support in the House or Senate.</p><p>After the bill&#39;s passage, GOP Senate Minority Leader Mitch McConnell of Kentucky <a href=\"https://www.republicanleader.senate.gov/newsroom/research/a-classic-example-of-big-government-democratic-overreach\">slammed</a> the legislation as &#34;a classic example of big-government Democratic overreach in the name of Covid relief&#34; and &#34;one of the worst pieces of legislation&#34; he&#39;s seen in his 36 years in the Senate.</p><p>He also <a href=\"https://www.politico.com/video/2021/03/10/mcconnell-covid-relief-bill-worst-legislation-160339\">said</a> the GOP would &#34;talk repeatedly&#34; to the American public about the true contents of the bill in the coming months.</p><p>However, some Republicans are now touting popular elements of the bill they railed against on Capitol Hill.</p><p>Conservative freshman GOP Rep. Madison Cawthorn of North Carolina <a href=\"https://twitter.com/RepCawthorn/status/1376974227753070593\">pointed to health funding</a> in his district in a tweet last week, including nearly $2.5 million for the Appalachian Mountain Community Health Centers and $4.6 million for Western North Carolina Community Health Services that was part of the legislation.</p><p>&#34;Happy to announce that NC-11 was awarded grants from the U.S. Department of Health &#38; Human Services,&#34; he wrote. &#34;Proud to see tax-payer dollars returned to NC-11.&#34;</p><p>Democratic National Committee Chairman Jaime Harrison <a href=\"https://twitter.com/harrisonjaime/status/1377014594267398145\">took note</a> of Hawthorn&#39;s tweet and blasted the congressman and the GOP.</p><p>&#34;Come&#39;on man,&#34; he wrote. &#34;<a href=\"https://twitter.com/RepCawthorn\" data-focusable=\"true\">@RepCawthorn</a> is trying to take credit for the grants HE VOTED AGAINST. Republicans have no shame.&#34;</p><blockquote class=\"twitter-tweet blockquote\" data-lang=\"en\" data-cards=\"\" data-conversation=\"\">-Jaime Harrison, DNC Chair  (@harrisonjaime) <a href=\"https://twitter.com/mims/statuses/1377014594267398145?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw\">March 30, 2021</a></blockquote><script async=\"\" src=\"//platform.twitter.com/widgets.js\" charset=\"utf-8\"></script><p><strong><em>Read more: </em></strong><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/issues-that-could-tank-bidens-infrastructure-plan-congress-salt-taxes-2021-4\"><em>Here are 9 hurdles Biden&#39;s infrastructure plan would have to overcome in Congress before it can become law</em></a></p><p>Cawthorn spokesman Micah Bock <a href=\"https://www.nbcnews.com/politics/congress/republicans-trumpet-elements-covid-19-relief-bill-they-voted-against-n1262626\">told NBC News</a> in a statement last week that the congressman uses his social media account &#34;to post information relevant to his constituents in NC-11.&#34;</p><p>&#34;Oftentimes this means providing relevant federal information on proposals that the congressman does not support,&#34; he said. &#34;There are portions of the American Rescue Plan that benefit NC-11, however, bills are not passed in portions, they are passed entirely or not at all, and this bill does significantly more harm than good.&#34;</p><p>GOP Sen. Roger Wicker of Mississippi <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/wicker-praises-covid-19-relief-funding-after-voting-against-bill-2021-3\">praised</a> the billions in targeted funding for the restaurant industry that he championed - it was part the final package that he voted against.</p><p>&#34;Independent restaurant operators have won $28.6 billion worth of targeted relief,&#34; <a href=\"https://twitter.com/SenatorWicker/status/1369770036982915084\">he tweeted</a> after the bill passed. &#34;This funding will ensure small businesses can survive the pandemic by helping to adapt their operations and keep their employees on the payroll.&#34;</p><p>When asked by CNN&#39;s Manu Raju why he didn&#39;t support the full measure, Wicker said he didn&#39;t have to accept the full measure and was critical of the questioning.</p><p>&#34;Just because there&#39;s one good provision in a $1.9 trillion bill, doesn&#39;t mean I have to vote for it ... I think it&#39;s a stupid question. I&#39;m not going to vote for $1.9 trillion just because it has a couple of good provisions in it.&#34;</p><p>Congressional Republicans have currently found themselves boxed into a corner on the issue.</p><p>A Pew Research poll <a href=\"https://www.pewresearch.org/politics/2021/03/09/broad-public-support-for-coronavirus-aid-package-just-a-third-say-it-spends-too-much/\">released</a> shortly before the bill&#39;s signing showed 70% of US adults backing the legislation, with only 28% of respondents opposed to the measure.</p><p>Even 41% of Republican or Republican-leaning respondents, a significant minority, backed the COVID-19 relief bill.</p><p>National GOP leaders have pledged to use the bill as a campaign attack against Democrats in the 2022 midterm elections, but nearly three dozen Republican mayors across the county, from David Holt of Oklahoma City to John Giles of Mesa, <a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/gop-mayors-support-coronavirus-relief-bill-biden-stimulus-economy-2021-2\">backed</a> the legislation.</p><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article src=\"https://i.insider.com/60633a1f67187800184ad483?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure><ul class=\"summary-list\">\n<li>PS, the private terminal at LAX, has been a haven for wealthy travelers looking to avoid the traveling public.</li>\n<li>As a result, memberships have been surging as the wealthy want a more private experience.</li>\n<li>I visited a newly redesigned suite and saw first-hand what they&#39;re paying thousands of dollars for. </li>\n<li id=\"recirc\"><a href=\"https://www.businessinsider.com/?hprecirc-bullet\">See more stories on Insider&#39;s business page</a>.</li>\n</ul>\n<div id=\"slideshow\">\n\tPS opened in 2017 as the Private Suite, a one-of-a-kind private terminal at one of the country's busiest airports. Like most travel and hospitality companies, business was down at the pandemic's peak in 2020 as would-be travelers stayed at home amid lockdowns.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338d067187800184ad470?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tBut just over one full year since lockdowns began, PS is reporting a resurgence in new memberships from flyers getting ready to travel.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60635c6367187800184ad570?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS (Private Suite) at LAX\" height=\"1285\" width=\"1714\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>PS at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">PS at LAX</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tAmina Belouizdad, PS' co-chief executive officer, told Insider that memberships have surged and the company has signed on more new members than it had before the pandemic. Annual membership costs $4,500 but the wealthy are scooping them up, even if they don't have upcoming travel planned.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60636267c9d73b00186e9353?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS (Private Suite) at LAX\" height=\"1247\" width=\"1662\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>PS at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">PS at LAX</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\t\"I think people want to have peace of mind that they have access to this,\" Belouizdad said. \"It's a signal of customer sentiment, is what it is. People are saying, 'I'm expecting to travel over the next year, I want to make sure me and my family can do it safely.'\"\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/6063627967187800184ad588?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS (Private Suite) at LAX\" height=\"1666\" width=\"2223\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>PS at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">PS at LAX</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tAnd with that in mind, PS is embarking on a redesign for its Los Angeles flagship terminal to welcome back travelers with a new look. I stopped by PS on a recent layover in Los Angeles, here's what it was like.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60634f2dc9d73b00186e92d8?format=jpeg\" alt=\"Flying on Alaska Airlines during pandemic\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Flying on Alaska Airlines during the pandemic\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tThe major appeal of PS is avoiding the commercial terminal at LAX entirely, and that's only increased during the pandemic. Memberships are up as the wealthy want guaranteed access, even if they don't have plans to fly in the near future.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338c867187800184ad46a?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tFor those arriving at LAX by plane, the experience starts with a chauffeured car. PS representatives wait in the jetway to meet guests as soon as they step off of their flights, and promptly escort them to an awaiting vehicle below.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b9fdd106eb50019d05737?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Direct\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tPS has a fleet of vehicles available to use depending on group size but the flagship is the BMW 750i. Ideal for one to two passengers, the classic all-white sedan features an executive configuration for passengers in the back.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b9fde106eb50019d05738?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Direct\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tThe car is loaded with luxurious amenities including leather seats with recline functionality to individual climate control for passengers in the back.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b9fdf0d155e0019ef691c?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Direct\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tThere are even seat-back entertainment screens from which the SiriusXM radio can be controlled.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338dac9d73b00186e923e?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tThen, it's around a 10 to 15-minute drive to PS, located on the south side of the airport.  As two runways separate the facility from the commercial terminals, drivers have to go all the way around the airport while obeying the airport's modest speed limit\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b9fe10d155e0019ef691f?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Direct\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tAs an aviation enthusiast, however, I wish the drive lasted longer as we were right alongside moving aircraft for most of the drive.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/605b9fe00d155e0019ef691d?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Direct\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tBehemoth jets like the Boeing 747 were just outside the window, departing and landing just feet from the car.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338cb67187800184ad46c?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tIt was like getting a private tour of the airport all while traveling at the height of luxury.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/60634013c9d73b00186e926c?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1726\" width=\"2301\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tUpon arrival at PS, it's just a short walk down a private hallway into the facility. Everything from reservations to payment is done online so there's no checking in or waiting in line. I didn't even see another guest for the entirety of my stay.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338d0c9d73b00186e9232?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tThere are 13 suites in total at PS. Not all have received the redesign but that project is expected to be completed within the next six months.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338d767187800184ad477?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tI walked into the suite and felt as if I'd just checked into a luxury hotel.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338dac9d73b00186e923c?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tIt was incredibly modern and above any private lounge that I've seen at an airport. Members pay $3,250 per visit while non-members pay $4,350 per visit for up to four travelers.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338ca67187800184ad46b?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tThe suites aren't as large as a hotel suite but are comparable in size to a New York City studio apartment and include spacious living areas, wet bars, fully-stocked mini-fridges, and private bathrooms, among other features.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338d6c9d73b00186e9238?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tPS takes a personal touch when dealing with guests. A handwritten note is left for guests welcoming them to the facility and detailing what they can expect from the stay.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338ddc9d73b00186e9240?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tA massive high-definition television with DirecTV serves as the main entertainment for the suite, helping pass the time until a flight.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338cfc9d73b00186e9231?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tGuests can also make use of the in-suite phone and stationary. PS staff use the phone to communicate with guests and keep them informed on their departure information.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338d567187800184ad476?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tThis quasi-kitchen and wet bar are where all of the suite's food and beverage items can be found.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338d6c9d73b00186e9239?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tA selection of high-end snacks, liquors, and wines were all on offer and available free of charge to guests.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338d9c9d73b00186e923b?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tSnacks included pistachios, almonds, keto-friendly cereal, and water crackers, to name just a few.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338d967187800184ad479?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tGuests are also encouraged to take snacks with them on the plane and given this blue box to do so.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338d767187800184ad478?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tThe fridge contained chilled soft drinks, waters, milk, alcoholic beverages, and even some more snacks. A guest here will truly want for nothing as everything is at their fingertips.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338dac9d73b00186e923d?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tThose making cocktails can use the bar station and the pre-filled bucket of ice.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338ddc9d73b00186e923f?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tAnd there was no shortage of glasses, cups, and dishes to use when dining.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338ce67187800184ad46d?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tComplimentary travel accessories were also scattered across the suite including noise-isolating headphones, headphone splitters, and charging cables.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338d4c9d73b00186e9237?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tThe luxury continued into the restroom complete with marble floors and vanities, as well as gold-plated sink faucets.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338cec9d73b00186e9230?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tAnd the complimentary amenities kept on coming with everything a traveler would need to freshen up before a flight.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338ccc9d73b00186e922e?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tThere was even a selection of over-the-counter medications on offer if a traveler is feeling unwell or just wants a dose of Vitamin C to boost the immune system while traveling.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338d3c9d73b00186e9236?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tThe suite design is the result of a partnership with Cliff Fong, a renowned design consultant, and it really felt like home instead of a transient space.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338d1c9d73b00186e9234?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\t\"Our vision was always like, let's create a space that feels residential, that feels like their home, that doesn't feel like the airport, that doesn't feel like a commercial space, that feels very familiar and collected,\" Belouizdad said.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338d267187800184ad473?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tThe suite window overlooked the airfield, as well as the PS fleet of luxury vehicles. The firm also offers a new service, called PS Direct, where flyers can be taken straight from their domestic flights to their final destination and avoid both the commercial terminal and the PS facility altogether.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338cf67187800184ad46f?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1874\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tDirectly adjacent to the suite is an outdoor patio with benches and chairs to enjoy a bit of the outdoors before heading off on a plane for however many hours.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338d967187800184ad47a?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tSuite 13 is often the most sought after since it includes this private outdoor space, accessible via a sliding door from the living room.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338da67187800184ad47b?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tMeals are included in the stay and everything comes pre-packaged for sanitary reasons.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338d8c9d73b00186e923a?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tThe current menu is largely focused on Los Angeles-inspired meals, mainly salads and sandwiches, for lunch and dinner.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338d467187800184ad475?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tI sampled the Peruvian steak sandwich and the chicken and prosciutto salad. Both were bursting with flavor and better than most of what's available even in LAX's premium lounges.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338d1c9d73b00186e9233?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tIt really came as no surprise that the wealthy are buying up access to the facility since staying here was so much more enjoyable than any airport experience I've had in years.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338da67187800184ad47c?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tFor me, I found the true luxury of the suite wasn't the complimentary goodies that were offered but that it was a quiet place to relax during a long layover nestled into an already long day of travel. Suites also feature a sleep kit with eyeshades and earplugs.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338ddc9d73b00186e9241?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tWhen it was time to leave, PS staff came to the suite and escorted me to the in-house Transportation and Security Administration checkpoint. There's no line and TSA PreCheck was available.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338ce67187800184ad46e?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n\tThen, it was just a short drive back to the commercial terminals and my awaiting JetBlue Airways flight.\n\t<figure>\n\t<img src=\"https://i.insider.com/606338d2c9d73b00186e9235?format=jpeg\" alt=\"PS Private Terminal at LAX\" height=\"1875\" width=\"2500\" charset=\"\">\n<figcaption>Visiting PS, the private terminal at Los Angeles International Airport.\n<p class=\"copyright\">Thomas Pallini/Insider</p>\n</figcaption>\n</figure>\n\t\n</div><div class=\"read-original\">Read the original article on <a
